      momoj(function(){
        momoj(window).scroll(function(){
          var topval = momoj("body").scrollTop();
          //判斷捲軸是否超過主選單，如超過主選單，將主選單固定至天的位置，方便點擊時呈現 
          if (document.documentElement.scrollTop > 0 || topval > 0) {
            momoj("#bt_0_layout_b250").attr("style","z-index:6");
            //當捲軸離開頂時,將搜尋歸位,然後把商城跟下載App的按鈕隱藏 
            momoj(".searchArea").removeClass("tips");
            momoj(".momomallBtn, .appDownloadbtn").hide();       
            return;
          } else {
            momoj("#bt_0_layout_b250").removeAttr("style");
            momoj(".searchArea").addClass("tips");
            momoj(".momomallBtn, .appDownloadbtn").show(); 
            return;
          }
        });
      });
    </script>

      <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
          momoj(document).ready(function () {
            momoj('#keyword').KeywordSearch();
          });
          momoj('#keyword').bind('focus',function(){
            momoj(this).addClass('now');
          }).bind('blur',function(){
            if(momoj.trim(momoj(this).val())==''){
              momoj(this).removeClass('now');
            }
          });

          function search(){
            var keyWord = momoj('#keyword').val();
			keyWord = keyWord.replaceAll('<', '').replaceAll('>', '').replaceAll('\'', '').replaceAll('\"', '');
			momoj('#keyword').val(keyWord);
            var cateCode = momoj('#p_lgrpCode').val();
             var couponSeq = momoj('#couponSeqTxt').val();
            var couponName = momoj('#couponNameTxt').val();
            var isconstriction = momoj('#keyword').attr("isconstriction");
            var switchconstriction = momoj('#keyword').attr("switchconstriction");
            var originalCateCode = momoj('#originalCateCode').val();
            var cateType = momoj('#cateType').val();
            var isBrandCategory = momoj('#isBrandCategory').val();
            if(keyWord == ''){
              if(typeof isconstriction == "undefined" || isconstriction =="false"){
                var randomKeyword = momoj('#keyword').attr('placeholder');
                if(randomKeyword != '' && randomKeyword !='請輸入關鍵字或品號'){
                  keyWord = randomKeyword;
                  momoj('#keyword').val(randomKeyword);
                }else {
                  alert('請輸入關鍵字或品號');
                  return false;
                }
              }else{
                alert('請輸入關鍵字或品號');
                return false;
              }
            }
            
            if(isFinite(keyWord) && (keyWord.length >= 6 && keyWord.length<= 10)){
              cateCode = '';
            }
            var url ='';
            if(typeof switchconstriction == "undefined" || switchconstriction=="false" ){
            if( typeof couponSeq !='undefined' && couponSeq != null && couponSeq != '') {
                url = "/search/searchShop.jsp?keyword=" + encodeURIComponent(keyWord) + "&couponSeq=" +  encodeURIComponent(couponSeq)+ "&couponName=" +  encodeURIComponent(couponName);
              }else { 
                url = "/search/searchShop.jsp?keyword=" + encodeURIComponent(keyWord) ;
              }
            }else{
              url = "/search/searchShop.jsp?keyword=" + encodeURIComponent(keyWord)  + "&originalCateCode=" +  encodeURIComponent(originalCateCode)+ "&cateType=" +  encodeURIComponent(cateType)+ "&isBrandCategory=" +  encodeURIComponent(isBrandCategory);
            }
            location.href = url;
          };
      </script>

momoj('ul.leftMenu li, ul.rightMenu li').delegate('a', 'click', function(){
  var title = momoj(this).attr('title');
  if(title.length > 0){
    'object'===typeof ArkModule&&ArkModule.track&&(
      ArkModule.track('btn_click', {
        $page_name: location.pathname,
        btn_location: 'top',
        btn_name: title ? title : 'none'
      })
    );
  }
});

  var searchKey = momoj('input[id=keyword]').val();
  searchKey = searchKey
    .replaceAll('<','')
    .replaceAll('>','')
    .replaceAll('\'','')
    .replaceAll('\"','');
  momoj('input[id=keyword]').val(searchKey);
  var has_result = true;
  var is_hot_word = false; 
  var is_recommended = false; 
  'object'===typeof ArkModule&&ArkModule.track&&(
    ArkModule.track('search',{
      key_word: searchKey,
      has_result: has_result,
      is_hot_word: is_hot_word,
      is_recommended: is_recommended
    })
  );
});

function getGclid() {
  return new URLSearchParams(window.location.search).get('gclid');
}

var gtagIdLabel = function(event, product_seller) {
  var _rtn = momoj.ajaxTool({
    data : {
      flag : 5011,
      webBrandNo  : product_seller,
      event: event
    }
  });
  if((_rtn && _rtn.rtnCode === 200)) {
    return _rtn.rtnData.data;
  } else {
    return [];
  }
}

function getGTag(event, prodInfo) {
  var gclid = getGclid();

  if(typeof gclid == 'undefined'||gclid == null||gclid.trim().length == 0){
    return {};
  }
  console.log("gclid:" + gclid);

  var remarketingPrice = momoj('.prdPrice li').last().find('span').first().text().replace(/,/g,'');
  var quantity = prodInfo.product_quantity;
  
  var idLabelArr = gtagIdLabel(event, prodInfo.product_seller);
  
  var gtagARR = [];
  momoj.each(idLabelArr, function(k,v){
      var g = {
      event: event + "M2",
      product_id: prodInfo.product_id,
      product_name: prodInfo.product_name,
      product_seller: prodInfo.product_seller,
      product_value: remarketingPrice * prodInfo.product_quantity,
      product_quantity: prodInfo.product_quantity,
      product_currency: prodInfo.product_currency,
      transaction_id: event + ""+ new Date().getTime(),
      conversion_id: v.conversion_id,
      conversion_label: v.conversion_label
      };
      gtagARR.push(g);
  });
  return gtagARR;
}

  //2011.06.03 tonychen
  function addGoodsChk(work) {
    for (var v = 0; v < 10; v++){
      if (document.getElementById('dschb' + v) != null) {
        
        
        if (document.getElementById('listGoodsWork' + v).value.search(work)<0 
            || document.getElementById('dsc' + v).value != document.productForm.receipt_flag.value 
            || document.getElementById('addBuyChk' + v).value == 'disabled') {
          
          var isOK = false;
          
          if(document.productForm.receipt_flag.value=='10'
              && document.getElementById('dsc' + v).value=='10'
              && /first|shopcar/.test(work)
              && /first|shopcar/.test(document.getElementById('listGoodsWork' + v).value)
              && document.getElementById('addBuyChk' + v).value != 'disabled') {
            isOK = true;
          }
          if (isOK) {
            document.getElementById('dschb' + v).disabled=false;
          } else {
            document.getElementById('dschb' + v).checked=false;
            document.getElementById('dschb' + v).disabled=true;
          }

        } else {
          document.getElementById('dschb' + v).disabled=false;
        }
      }
    }
  }
  
  function changeDelyWork(delyWorkId) {

    function getCoupon(curPage){
      var salePrice = '1690';
      var salePriceStr = '1,690';
      if(couopnList != null && couopnList != "" && couopnList != "undefined"){
        var couponTotRow = couopnList.length;
        var str = '<p class="promotePrice">商品促銷價<b>' + salePriceStr + '</b>元</p>';
        str += '<div class="couponListRow">折價劵適用促銷價折抵，無法與活動同時折抵</div>';
        str += '<div class="couponList"><table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">';
        str += '<thead><tr><th>折價券名稱</th><th>折價券面額</th><th>折價後金額</th></tr></thead>';
        str += '<tbody>';
        for(var i = 0;i<couponTotRow && i<pageRow;i++){
          var singleList = couopnList[i];
          var startDate = singleList.CP_SDATE;
          var endDate = singleList.CP_EDATE;
          var cpName = singleList.CP_NAME;
          var cpPrice = singleList.CP_PRICE;
          var cpLastPriceStr = singleList.CP_LAST_PRICE_STRING;
          str += '<tr><td class="couponName"><span>' + startDate + " ~ " + endDate + '</span>' + cpName + "</td>";
          str += '<td>' + cpPrice +'</td><td class="finalPrice">$<b>' + cpLastPriceStr + '</b></td></tr>';
        }
        str += '</tbody></table></div>';
        var couponInfoStr = '<ol><li>以上金額依您帳戶內可使用的折價券面額計算</li><li>折價券適用促銷價金額折抵，實際折抵金額以購物車結帳頁面為準！</li><li>欲使用折價劵，請至購物車選用</li></ol>';
        couponAreaShow(str,couponInfoStr);
      }else{
        var data = {
            data: {URL:"/ajax/ajaxTool.jsp?rn=" + Math.random(),flag:2016,
              "lGroup":'05',"mGroup":'03',
              "sGroup":'07',"dGroup":'03',
              "goodsCode":'11289042',"salePrice":salePrice,
              "pageRow":pageRow,"curPage":curPage,"setYn":'0',
              "webBrandNo":'20170905113302164',"entpCode":'018460'
            }
        }
        
        
        var _rtnData = momoj.ajaxTool(data);
        if(_rtnData.rtnCode == "200"){
          var rtnData = _rtnData.rtnData;
          var str = '<p class="promotePrice">商品促銷價<b>' + salePriceStr + '</b>元</p>';
          if(rtnData.rtnChk == "non_login"){//使用者未登入
            momoj('.usableCoupon .couponInfo ul').html("");
            str += '<div class="noCoupon">請先登入，以查詢可使用的折價券</div>';
          }else if(rtnData.rtnChk == "ok"){
            couopnList = rtnData.list;
            if(couopnList != null && couopnList != "" && couopnList != "undefined"){
              getCoupon(1);
              return;
            }else{
              str += '<div class="noCoupon">很抱歉，帳戶內查無本商品可使用的折價券</div>';
            }
          }else{
            str += '<div class="noCoupon">很抱歉，帳戶內查無本商品可使用的折價券</div>';
          }
          var couponInfoStr = '';
          if(rtnData.rtnChk != "non_login"){
            couponInfoStr = '<ol><li>以上金額依您帳戶內可使用的折價券面額計算</li><li>折價券適用促銷價金額折抵，實際折抵金額以購物車結帳頁面為準！</li><li>欲使用折價劵，請至購物車選用</li></ol>';
          }
          couponAreaShow(str,couponInfoStr);
        }else{
          alert("很抱歉!伺服器暫時無法連線，請稍候再試，或連繫本公司客服人員處理。");
        }
      }
    }

        momoj('.vendordetailview.specification').nextAll().remove();
        var p = momoj('.vendordetailview.specification').parent();
        while (p.length > 0 && p[0].tagName != 'BODY') {
          p.prevAll().not('link,script').remove();
          p.nextAll().not('link,script').remove();
          p = p.parent();
        }        
      }, 1000)
    } else if (location.hash == '#gifts') {
    var html = '';
    //if (momoj('.prdwarp .prdimgArea .preferential i').length > 0) {
    //momoj('.prdwarp .prdimgArea .preferential .tip, .prdwarp .prdimgArea .preferential .giftInfo').each(function(i, tip){
    //  if (momoj(tip).text() == '查看贈品') {
    //  tip.click();
    //  html += momoj('.showgiftsList:first').parent().html();
    //  momoj('.showgiftsList:first').parent().remove();
    //  }
    //});     
    //}
    
      //vendordetailview giftsArea
      if (momoj('.vendordetailview.giftsArea').length > 0) {
    //html += '<ul class="vendordetailmenu">';
        //html += '<li class="selected"><span>贈品</span></li>';
        //html += '</ul>';
    if (momoj('.vendordetailview.giftsArea p').text() != '') {
      html += '<div class="vendordetailview giftsArea">';
          html += momoj('.vendordetailview.giftsArea').html();
      html += '</div>';
    }
      }
      
      setTimeout(function() {

      var promo = (momoj('.prdwarp .prdimgArea .preferential i').length > 0);
      momoj('body').children().hide();
      if (html != '') {
      momoj('body').append(html);
      } else {
      if (promo) {
        momoj('body').append("<span>活動贈品</span>");
      } else {
        momoj('body').append("<span>無贈品</span>");
            }
      }   
      
        }, 1000)

    }
  //瀏覽記錄
    var data = {data:{URL:"/ajax/ajaxTool.jsp?rn=" + Math.random(), 
                flag:2028,
                "goodsCode":11289042,
                }}
    momoj.ajaxTool(data);
    //商品頁瀏覽記錄
    var data = {data:{URL:"/ajax/ajaxTool.jsp?rn=" + Math.random(), 
                flag:2029                               
                }}
    var _rtnData = momoj.ajaxTool(data);
    if (_rtnData.rtnCode == "200") {
        if (_rtnData.rtnData.result!='') {
          momoj('.recordArea ul').append(_rtnData.rtnData.result);                    
       }
    }
    //判斷開賣中商品,先取google recapcha token
    var switchType = momoj('#saleNoticeSwitchType').val();
    if(typeof switchType != 'undefined' && switchType =="2"){
      momoj("#commonGtoken").setGtoken("add_cart");//google recaptcha
    }
    
  funcSameDate.init();
  //產生商品評分
  //判斷開關關起來,則不顯示商品評分和總銷售量區塊
  if(momoj("#isSwitchGoodsReviews").val() =="1" || momoj("#isSwitchGoodsTotalSales").val() =="1" ){
    var isSwitchGoodsReviews = momoj("#isSwitchGoodsReviews").val()||'';
    var isSwitchGoodsTotalSales = momoj("#isSwitchGoodsTotalSales").val()||'';
    var goodsCanReviews = momoj("#goodsCanReviews").val()||''
    goodsReviews.getGoodsReviews(momoj("#goods_code").val(), goodsCanReviews, isSwitchGoodsReviews, isSwitchGoodsTotalSales);
    goodsComment.init();
  }
});

//針對IE瀏覽器重新設定專推的iframe height屬性
function resizeVendordetailview(){ 
  var _userAgent = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
  //IE10以前只需判斷有無包含msie字樣，IE11後已經不同了，要判斷trident 跟 11字樣，又因為IE 11是末代所以先寫死
  if(_userAgent.indexOf("msie")>-1||(_userAgent.indexOf("trident")>-1&&_userAgent.indexOf("11")>-1)){
    setTimeout(function(){momoj('#ifrmGoods').attr('height',momoj('#ifrmGoods').contents().find('body').attr('scrollHeight'));},2000);
  }
}
function addGoodsBuyInfo(addGoodsSeq) {
  var addGoodsSum = 0;
  var totalCount = document.getElementById('count').value;
  var addGoodsRadio = totalCount * document.getElementById('ratiod' + addGoodsSeq).value;
  for (var v = 0; v < 10; v++){
    var chkAddCountDschbV = document.getElementById('dschb' + v);
    if (chkAddCountDschbV != null && chkAddCountDschbV.checked == true) {
      addGoodsSum += document.getElementById('dsgno' + v).value * 1;
    }
  }
  if (addGoodsSum != 0) {
    if (addGoodsSum > addGoodsRadio) {
      alert('主商品購買數量' + totalCount + '只能加價購買' + addGoodsRadio + '個商品');
    }
  }
}
function chaddGoodsNum(addGoodsSeq) {
  var addgoodsdt = momoj('#dsgc'+ addGoodsSeq +' :selected').val();
  var addgoodsdt_num = momoj('#dt_num'+addGoodsSeq + '_' + addgoodsdt).val();
  momoj('#dsgno'+ addGoodsSeq +' option').remove();
  for (var i = 1; i <=addgoodsdt_num; i++){
    momoj('#dsgno'+ addGoodsSeq).append('<option value="'+i+'">'+i+'</option>');
  }
}

function changeAddGoodsPic(oThis){
  var container = momoj(oThis);
  var imgUrl = container.find("option:selected").attr("imgUrl")
  if(!!imgUrl && imgUrl != ""){
    var img = container.parents("li").find("img");
    img.attr("src",imgUrl);
  }
}

function addGoodsOrderNote(oThis){
  var container = momoj(oThis);
  var goodsPaymentDesc = container.find("option:selected").attr("goodsPaymentDesc");
  if(goodsPaymentDesc){
    var preordernote = container.parents("li").find("span.prd-pre-order-note");
    preordernote.text(goodsPaymentDesc);
  }
}
/** 彈出視窗時的黑透明背景 **/
function bkArea() {
  var bodywidth = momoj("body")[0].clientWidth; /** 將整個body的寬度置入bodywidth **/
  var bodyheight = momoj("body")[0].clientHeight; /** 將整個body的高度置入bodyheight **/
  momoj(".fancybox-overlay").css({"width":+ bodywidth+"px","height":+bodyheight+"px"}).fadeTo("slow",0.5); /** 將body的寬高置入此層，然後淡出透明度0.5 **/
}


var cur_quality = '';
function PlayClick(quality) {
  var player=document.getElementById('video');
  var image=document.getElementById('goodsimg');
  var mediaPlayer = document.getElementById('MediaPlayer');
  if  (quality != "" && cur_quality!=quality) {
    image.style.display = 'none';
    player.style.display = 'block';
    mediaPlayer.detachEvent('PlayStateChange',checkPlayStatus);
    mediaPlayer.fileName='mms://vod.momoshop.com.tw/42/11289042_' + quality + '.wmv';
    mediaPlayer.play();
    cur_quality=quality;
  }
}
function checkPlayStatus(oldState,newState) {
  var mediaPlayer = document.getElementById('MediaPlayer');
  try {
    if (mediaPlayer.PlayState==0) {
      video.style.display = 'none';
      goodsimg.style.display = 'block';
      cur_quality="";
    }
  } catch (e) {}
}

function ZoomImage(img,bFlag,imgB,index) {
  if(bFlag=='1'){
    //有放大圖
    momoj("#goodsimgB").show();
    momoj("#goodsimgNB").hide();
    momoj("#goodsimg a").eq(0).attr("href",imgB);
    momoj("#goodsimgB .jqzoom img").eq(0).attr("src",img);
    momoj(".zoomimg").show();
    jQuery('.jqzoom').jqzoom({
        zoomType: 'reverse',
        lens:true,
        preloadImages: false,
        alwaysOn:false
    });
  }else{
    //沒有放大圖
    momoj("#goodsimgB").hide();
    momoj("#goodsimgNB").show();
    momoj("#goodsimgNB .nojqzoom img").eq(0).attr("src",img);
    momoj(".zoomimg").hide();
  }
  
  //只有第一張圖才顯示圓標圖和上下標
  if(index == 0){
    momoj("#goodsimgB .gmclass .imgTag img").show();
    momoj("#goodsimgB .gmclass .imgTagRectangle img").show();
    momoj("#goodsimgB .gmclass .imgTagBottom img").show();
    momoj("#goodsimgB .gmclass .ec-tag-official img").show();
  }else{
    momoj("#goodsimgB .gmclass .imgTag img").hide();
    momoj("#goodsimgB .gmclass .imgTagRectangle img").hide();
    momoj("#goodsimgB .gmclass .imgTagBottom img").hide();
    momoj("#goodsimgB .gmclass .ec-tag-official img").hide();
  }
  
  StopClick();
}

function isDelyFlag6() {
  var categoryCode = "1000700002";
  return categoryCode === "4000300002" || categoryCode === "1000700004";
}

function isDelyFlag11(){
  var entpCode = momoj('[name=entp_code]').val();
  return entpCode === "013364" || entpCode === "021002" || entpCode === "014453";
}

//是否商品分類是服飾分類
function isOutfit() {
  var categoryCode = "1000700002" || '';
  var catesub = categoryCode.substr(0,2);
  return catesub === "19";
}


function checkGoodsDtDliDay(firstLoad){
  var _firstLoad = firstLoad || '';	
  
  var checkC = momoj('#goodsdt_code').val();
  var isSaleNotice = momoj('#isSaleNotice').val();
  var _showGdsDt = momoj('#ShowGoodsDt');
  var goodsDtCnt = momoj('#goodsDtCount_' + checkC).val();
  var entpCode = momoj('[name=entp_code]').val();
  var msg = "&nbsp";
  if(window.isFiveHour && (delyInfo.delyTemp === "02" || delyInfo.delyTemp === "03")) {
    _showGdsDt.html(getDelyFlagMsg(12));
  } else if(window.isFiveHour) {
    _showGdsDt.html(getDelyFlagMsg(10));
  } else if(checkC == '0' || goodsDtCnt==0) {
    if(!isSaleNotice){
      _showGdsDt.html(msg);
    }
  }else{
    if(!isSaleNotice){
      var delyFlag = parseInt(momoj('#' + checkC).attr('delyFlag'));
      var delyNo = parseInt(momoj('#' + checkC).attr('delyNo'));
      var delyCount = momoj('#' + checkC).attr('delyCount');
      var from = momoj('#' + checkC).attr('delyFrom');
      var end = momoj('#' + checkC).attr('delyEnd');
      var _checkC = checkC || '';
    
      var delyType = momoj('#delyType').val();
      var isShop12H = momoj('#shop12hYn').val() == '1';
      
      if(delyType=='10' && !isShop12H) {
        momoj('#dely_end').val(end);
      }
      
      msg = getDelyFlagMsg(delyFlag, delyNo, delyCount, from, end);
	  var showGoodsDt = momoj("#ShowGoodsDt").html();
      _showGdsDt.html(msg);	
	  
	  if(_firstLoad == '1'){ //一載入文案改成如果多規格就不寫入讓原本一載入最大區間文案顯示      
		if((showGoodsDt.indexOf('此為預購商品，預計') > -1) && (msg.indexOf('此為預購商品，預計') > -1)){
		  _showGdsDt.html(showGoodsDt);	
		}
		
		if((showGoodsDt.indexOf('付款完成後，預計') > -1) && (msg.indexOf('付款完成後，預計') > -1)){
		  _showGdsDt.html(showGoodsDt);	
		}
		
		if((momoj("#spec1 li.selected").length == 0) && showGoodsDt == "因商品屬性關係，將有專人與您約定送貨時間"){
      	  _showGdsDt.html("因商品屬性關係，將有專人與您約定送貨時間");	
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

function ValidCount(cnt, no, gb, gcode, yn, qty, rate, gift_qty) {
  var f = document.productForm;
  if (f.gift_promo_yn10.checked == true) {
    f.gipromo_no10.value = no;
    f.gift_gb10.value = gb;
    f.gift_goods_code10.value = gcode;
    f.gift_limit_yn10.value = yn;
    f.gift_limit_qty10.value = qty;
    f.gift_rate10.value = rate;
    f.gift_count10.value = gift_qty;
  } else {
    f.gipromo_no10.value = '';
    f.gift_gb10.value = '';
    f.gift_goods_code10.value = '';
    f.gift_limit_yn10.value = '';
    f.gift_limit_qty10.value = '';
    f.gift_rate10.value = '';
    f.gift_count10.value = '';
  }
  giftAutoChkSwitch = false;
}

function iframeOnload() {    
  momoj('.prdwarp .prdinformation').show();
  momoj('#ifrmGoods').attr('height', momoj('#ifrmGoods').contents().height());
  momoj('.prdwarp .prdinformation').hide();
  momoj("#ifrmGoods").contents().on("click", "a", onExternalLinkClick);
}

function isHttps(href) {
  return !!href && href.slice(0, 8) === "https://";
}

function isFuli(href) {
  return !!href && href.indexOf("www.momo5188.com") > 0;
}

function isInsert(href) {
  return !!href && href.indexOf("momoshop.com.tw") > 0 || href.indexOf("momo.dm") > 0 || href.indexOf("blog.momo") > 0 ;
}

function getAnchorElement(htmlElement) {
  return momoj(htmlElement).closest("A").get(0);  
}

function openNewTab(href) {
  window.open(href, "_blank");
}

function openExternalFloatingLayerBox(href) {
  floatingLayerBox({
    title: '', 
    boxwidth:1160,
    innerHtml:'<div class="iframeArea"><iframe src="' + href + '"></iframe></div>',
    id:'externalFloatingLayerBox',
    z_index:'7'
  });

  floatingLayerBoxAlignCenter();
}

function onExternalLinkClick(event) {
  var anchorElement = getAnchorElement(event.target);

  if(!anchorElement || !isHttps(anchorElement.href)) {
    event.preventDefault();
	alert("此為外部網站，部分功能無法正常瀏覽，目前不支援顯示，請您見諒");
    return;
  }

  if(isFuli(anchorElement.href)) {
    openNewTab(anchorElement.href);
    event.preventDefault();    
  } else if (isInsert(anchorElement.href)) {
    openNewTab(anchorElement.href);
    event.preventDefault();
  } else {
    openExternalFloatingLayerBox(anchorElement.href);
    event.preventDefault();
  }
}

}

  if(goods_set_yn == '1'){
    if(!isEverySpecSelected(momoj(".InSet"))){
      alert("請選擇商品規格");

  }});
  
}


function checkSetStock(){
  var goods_set_yn = momoj('[name=set_yn]').val();
  if(goods_set_yn == '1'){
    if(!isOneSet && momoj('.InSet').length == 0){
      checkSetGoodsDtCodePickHave();//可能出現沒InSet的狀況。
    }else if(isOneSet && momoj('.InSet').length == 0){
      checkSetGoodsDtCodePickHave();//set品單一子品,可能出現沒InSet的狀況。(若被中斷有可能沒有InSet)
    }
      
    momoj('.InSet').change(function(){//點擊set品的規格觸發事件
       if(momoj(this).find(":selected").val()!="na"){
           var setGoodDtOption = momoj(this).find('option:selected').attr("setGoodsDtPreOrderDesc"); // 獲取預購文案
           momoj(this).closest("li").find(".prd-info").text(setGoodDtOption).show(); //.prd-info set品的規格文案
         }else{
           momoj(this).closest("li").find(".prd-info").hide(); // 隱藏 .prd-info set品的規格文案
         }
      checkSetGoodsDtCodePickHave();
    }).trigger('change');//觸發改變規格圖(goodsSpecImg.js)
  }
}

function checkSetGoodsDtCodePickHave() {
  
  var isSwitch = momoj('#isSaleNotice').val();
  if( typeof isSwitch != 'undefined' && isSwitch != null && isSwitch != "" && isSwitch != "null"){
    momoj('#buy_no').hide();
    momoj('#inCar').hide();
    return;
  }
  if (document.getElementById('buy_yes') == null) {
    buyBtn = momoj('#buyBtnClick');
  } else {
    buyBtn = momoj('#buy_yes');
  }

  buyBtn.hide();                  
  momoj('#inCar').hide();         
  momoj('#ask_stock').hide();     
  momoj('#buy_no').hide();        
  momoj('#ask_1').hide();         

  if(momoj(".InSet").length > 0){
    var isSetOutOfStock = (isSomeSpecSoldOut(momoj(".InSet")) && isEverySpecSelected(momoj(".InSet"))
               || !isEverySpecSelected(momoj(".InSet")) && !salesYn);
    if(isSetOutOfStock) {
      if(canEverySpecAskStock(momoj(".InSet"))) {
        momoj('#buy_no').show();    
      } else {
        momoj('#ask_stock').show(); 
      }
    } else if(/^1$|^2$/.test(limitBuyInfo.restrictionType) && limitBuyInfo.rQty === 0) {
      momoj('#ask_stock').show(); 
    } else {
      buyBtn.show();                
      momoj('#inCar').show();       
    }
  }else{
    momoj('#ask_stock').show(); 
  }
}


function checkGoodsDtCodePickHave(obj){
  var goodsSaleYn = momoj("#salesYn").val();
  
  var isSwitch = momoj('#isSaleNotice').val();
  if( typeof isSwitch != 'undefined' && isSwitch != null && isSwitch != "" && isSwitch != "null"){
    momoj('#buy_no').hide();
    momoj('#inCar').hide();
    return;
  }else{
    var switchType = momoj('#saleNoticeSwitchType').val();
    var haveSaleNoticStock = momoj('#haveSaleNoticStock').val();
    if(typeof switchType != 'undefined' && switchType =="2" && haveSaleNoticStock=="N"){
      momoj('#ask_stock').show();//售完補貨中
      momoj('#buy_no').hide();//可訂購時通知我
      momoj('#buy_yes').hide();//直接購買
      momoj('#buyBtnClick').hide();//直接購買
      momoj('#inCar').hide();//加入購物車
      return;
    }
  }

  if (obj != null) {
    var buyBtn;
    if (document.getElementById('buy_yes') == null) {
      buyBtn = momoj('#buyBtnClick');
    } else {
      buyBtn = momoj('#buy_yes');
    }

    var goodsDtAmt = 0;
    var objAmt = obj.getAttribute("amt");
    if(objAmt && !isNaN(objAmt)) {  //佔量有可能為負值
      goodsDtAmt = parseInt(objAmt, 10);
      goodsDtAmt = goodsDtAmt > 0 ? goodsDtAmt : 0;
    }
    if (goodsDtAmt == 0) {
      if(goodsSaleYn){// 是否可以販售
        buyBtn.hide();
        momoj('#inCar').hide();
      }
      momoj('#buy_no').hide();
      momoj('#ask_stock').hide();
      var ask_stock = momoj("#goodsAskStockYn").val()||'';
      var ask_stock_arr = ask_stock.split(",");
      var ask_stock_yn = false;
      for (var i = 0; i < ask_stock_arr.length; i++) {
        if (ask_stock_arr[i].indexOf(obj.value) >= 0) {
          if (ask_stock_arr[i].indexOf('true') >= 0) {
            ask_stock_yn = true;
          }
        }
      }
      if (ask_stock_yn) {
        momoj('#buy_no').show();
      } else {
        momoj('#ask_stock').show();
      }
      return;
    } else if(/^1$|^2$/.test(limitBuyInfo.restrictionType) && goodsDtAmt > 0 && limitBuyInfo.rQty === 0) {
      buyBtn.hide();
      momoj('#inCar').hide();
      momoj('#ask_stock').show();
      momoj('#buy_no').hide();
      return;
    } else {
      if(goodsSaleYn){
        buyBtn.show();
        momoj('#inCar').show();
      }
      momoj('#buy_no').hide();
      momoj('#ask_stock').hide();
      
      momoj('#ask_1').hide();
    }
  }
}

function checkGoodsDtCodeSelectHave(obj){
  var goodsSaleYn = momoj("#salesYn").val();
  var ask_stock = momoj("#goodsAskStockYn").val()||'';
  var ask_stock_arr = ask_stock.split(",");
  var ask_stock_yn = false;
  var buyBtn;
  if (document.getElementById('buy_yes') == null) {
    buyBtn = document.getElementById('buyBtnClick');
  } else {
    buyBtn = document.getElementById('buy_yes');
  }
  if (obj != null) {
    if (obj.length > 1) {
      for (var m = 0; m < obj.length; m++) {
        if (obj[m].selected && obj[m].text.indexOf('(已售完)') >= 0) {
          for (var i = 0; i < ask_stock_arr.length; i++) {
            if (ask_stock_arr[i].indexOf(obj[m].value) >= 0) {
              if (ask_stock_arr[i].indexOf('true') >= 0) {
                ask_stock_yn = true;
              }
            }
          }
          momoj('#buy_no').hide();
          momoj('#ask_stock').hide();
          if (ask_stock_yn) {
            momoj("#buy_no").show();
            if(goodsSaleYn){// 是否可以販售
              buyBtn.style.display = 'none';
              momoj("#inCar").hide();
            }
            momoj("#ask_stock").hide();
          } else {
            if(goodsSaleYn){//是否可以販售
              buyBtn.style.display = 'none';
              momoj("#inCar").hide();
            }
            momoj("#ask_stock").show();
          }
          return ;
        } else {
          if(goodsSaleYn){
            buyBtn.style.display = '';
            momoj("#inCar").show();
          }
          momoj("#buy_no").hide();
          momoj("#ask_stock").hide();
          
          momoj("#ask_1").hide();
        }
        ask_stock_yn = false;
      }
    } else {
      if (obj.text.indexOf('(已售完)') >= 0) {
        for (var i = 0; i < ask_stock_arr.length; i++) {
          if (ask_stock_arr[i].indexOf(obj[m].value) >= 0) {
            if (ask_stock_arr[i].indexOf('true') >= 0) {
              ask_stock_yn = true;
            }
          }
        }
        momoj('#buy_no').hide();
        momoj('#ask_stock').hide();
        if (ask_stock_yn) {
          momoj("#buy_no").show();
          if(goodsSaleYn){//是否可以販售
            buyBtn.style.display = 'none';
            momoj("#inCar").hide();
          }
          momoj("#ask_stock").hide();
        } else {
          if(goodsSaleYn){//是否可以販售
            buyBtn.style.display = 'none';
            momoj("#inCar").hide();
          }
          momoj("#ask_stock").show();
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

function OrderProcess(work, goods_code, status) {  
  var _buyType = goods_code || '';
  buyType = _buyType;
  
  //開賣後10分鐘內的商品,未登入要強制登入
  var switchType = momoj('#saleNoticeSwitchType').val();
  if(typeof switchType != 'undefined' && switchType =="2"){
    momoj().MomoLogin({LoginSuccess:function(){
      doingOrderProcess(work, goods_code, status);
    }});
  }else if(is18Goods && !isYearAgreeAjax()){//分類頁來的在這判斷18禁
    check18Login();
    return;
  }else{
    doingOrderProcess(work, goods_code, status);
    }
}

function doingOrderProcess(work, goods_code, status) {
  if(!chgGoodsDtCode(true)){
    return false;
  }

  // 2023.10.04 hw2liao 贈險勾選檢查
  var hasInsurance = false;
  if(hasInsurance){
    if(!checkInsure()){
      return;
    }
  }
  var f = document.productForm;
  var useTwnTraCard = "0";

  if(f.chkUseTwnTraCard !=null && f.chkUseTwnTraCard.checked){
    useTwnTraCard = "1";
    momoj('#useTwnTraCard').val('1');
    // 2011.11.01 fhchen 國旅卡訂單限單1件商品，且商品數量須為1
    if(f.count.value > 1){
      var answer = confirm("提醒您！由於使用國民旅遊卡須獨立結帳，您選擇的此商品數量大於一件，\n系統只會將一件商品放入購物車。\n");
      if(answer){
        f.count.value = 1;
      }else{
        return;
      }
    }
    // 2011.11.01 fhchen 國旅卡訂單的配送方式須為一般甲配，也就是商品限放入[宅配]購物車
    if(!f.shopcart.checked){
      alert("商品配送方式異常，請聯絡客服人員！\n");
      return;
    }
  } else{
    useTwnTraCard = "0";
    momoj('#useTwnTraCard').val('0');
  }
  if (f.sale_price.value <= 0) {
    alert('商品異常，請聯絡客服人員');
    return ;
  }
  var saleCnt = 0;
  if (saleCnt > 0 && f.count.value > saleCnt) {
    getmsg('FA0065');
    return;
  }
  if (f.goodsdt_code.value == '0') {
    getmsg('FA0039');
    return;
  }
  if ('service' == 'admin') {
    getmsg("FA0041");
    return;
  }

  if (f.select_qty.value > 0) {
    var count = 0;
    if (typeof f.gipromo_no10.length != 'undefined') {
      for (var i = 0; i < f.gipromo_no10.length; i++) {
        if (giftAutoChkSwitch) {
          f.gift_promo_yn10[i].checked = true;
          ValidCount(f.gipromo_chkno10_forChk[i].value, f.gipromo_no10_forChk[i].value,
            f.gift_gb10_forChk[i].value, f.gift_goods_code10_forChk[i].value, f.gift_limit_yn10_forChk[i].value,
            f.gift_limit_qty10_forChk[i].value, f.gift_rate10_forChk[i].value, f.gift_count10_forChk[i].value);
        }
        if (f.gipromo_no10[i].value != '') count++;
      }
    } else {
      if (giftAutoChkSwitch) {
        f.gift_promo_yn10.checked = true;
        ValidCount(f.gipromo_chkno10_forChk.value, f.gipromo_no10_forChk.value,
          f.gift_gb10_forChk.value, f.gift_goods_code10_forChk.value, f.gift_limit_yn10_forChk.value,
          f.gift_limit_qty10_forChk.value, f.gift_rate10_forChk.value, f.gift_count10_forChk.value);
      }
      if (f.gipromo_no10.value != '') count++;
    }
    if (count > f.total_qty.value || count < f.total_qty.value) {
      alert(rtnmsg('FA0042').replace('X',f.select_qty.value));
      return;
    }
  }

  if ('00' != '00') {
    getmsg('FA0043');
    return;
  }
  
  f.work.value = '';
  if (f.dely_work.length > 1) {
    var delychked = true;
    for (var vr = 0; vr < f.dely_work.length; vr++) {
      if (f.dely_work[vr].checked) {
        f.work.value = f.dely_work[vr].value;
        delychked = false;
      }
    }
    if (delychked) {
      alert('沒有勾選');
      return;
    }
  } else {
    if (!f.dely_work.checked) {
      alert('沒有勾選');
      return;
    } else {
      f.work.value = f.dely_work.value;
    }
  }

  if ('false' == 'true' && 'true' == 'false') {
    if ('false' == 'true'){
      getmsg('FA0071');
      return;
    } else {
      getmsg('FE0051');
    }
  }

  if ('false' == 'true' && 'true' == 'true' && 'false' == 'true') {
    var pureBonus       = 11200;
    var cnt             = f.count.value
    var goodsBonus      = pureBonus * cnt ;
    var tempUsableBonus = 0;
    if (tempUsableBonus >= 0 && goodsBonus > tempUsableBonus) {
      getmsg("FA0069");
      return;
    }
  }

  if (f.dely_work.length > 1) {
    var msgStr = "";
    if(10 > 0){
      for (var v = 0; v < 10; v++){
        var chkAddGoodsDschbDi = document.getElementById('dschb'+v);
        var pTitleName = momoj('.prdwarp .increase li a')[v].innerText;       
        if (chkAddGoodsDschbDi != null && chkAddGoodsDschbDi.checked == true) {          
          if (document.getElementById('listGoodsWork' + v).value.search(f.work.value)<0 
              || document.getElementById('dsc' + v).value != document.productForm.receipt_flag.value 
              || document.getElementById('addBuyChk' + v).value == 'disabled') {
            
            var isOK = false;
            
            if (document.productForm.receipt_flag.value=='10'
                && document.getElementById('dsc' + v).value=='10'
                && /first|shopcar/.test(f.work.value)
                && /first|shopcar/.test(document.getElementById('listGoodsWork' + v).value)
                && document.getElementById('addBuyChk' + v).value != 'disabled') {
              isOK = true;
            }
            if (!isOK) {
              msgStr += pTitleName + "\n";  
            }
            
          }
        }
     }
     if(msgStr.length > 0){
       alert(msgStr + "不符合優惠加購條件!!");
       return ;
     }
    }
  }
  
  var addGoodsDtChk = true;
  if(10 > 0){
      for (var dv = 0; dv < 10; dv++){
        var chkAddGoodsDschbDi = document.getElementById('dschb'+dv);
        var pTitleName = momoj('.prdwarp .increase li a')[dv].innerText;       
        if (chkAddGoodsDschbDi != null && chkAddGoodsDschbDi.checked == true) {          
          var dsgc = document.getElementById('dsgc'+dv).value;
          if (dsgc == "") {
            addGoodsDtChk = false;
            break;
          }
        }
     }
     if(!addGoodsDtChk){
       alert("請選擇加購商品的規格。");
       return ;
     }
  }
  
  
  if(!funcSameDate.checkAndAlert()){//檢查統一出貨日
    return false;
  }
  

  var gosend='';
  var idno=0;
  var dsun=0;
  var availableAddGoodsSeq = 0;
  var addgoodsSwitch = false;
  for (var di=0;di < 10;di++){
    var chkAddGoodsDschbDi = document.getElementById('dschb'+di);
    if (chkAddGoodsDschbDi != null && chkAddGoodsDschbDi.checked == true) {
      availableAddGoodsSeq = di;
      if (idno == 0) {
        gosend+= document.getElementById('dtid'+di).value+':';
      } else {
        gosend+= ","+document.getElementById('dtid'+di).value+':';
      }
      gosend+=document.getElementById('dsgc'+di).value+':';
      gosend+=document.getElementById('dsgno'+di).value+':';
      gosend+=document.getElementById('adgopir'+di).value+':';
      gosend+=document.getElementById('dsa'+di).value+':';
      gosend+=document.getElementById('dsb'+di).value+':';
      gosend+=document.getElementById('dsc'+di).value+':';
      gosend+=document.getElementById('dsd'+di).value+':';
      gosend+=document.getElementById('dse'+di).value;
      dsun+=document.getElementById('dsgno'+di).value*1;
      idno++;
      addgoodsSwitch = true;
    }
  }
  if (addgoodsSwitch) {
    f.promo_type.value = '2';
    f.promo_types.value = '2';
  }
  document.getElementById('addgonumber').value = idno;
  document.getElementById('addgovalue').value = gosend;
  
  if (10!=0) {
    if (idno!=0) {
      var dscount = document.getElementById('count').value;
      var dsaddgono = dscount*document.getElementById('ratiod' + availableAddGoodsSeq).value;
      if (dsun > dsaddgono) {
        alert('主商品購買數量' + dscount + '只能加價購買' + dsaddgono + '個商品');
        return ;
      }
    }
  }

  var state = '';
  if (status == 'status_1') {
    state = '2';
  } else if (status == 'status_2') {
    state = f.status_2.value;
  }
  


  var goods_set_yn = momoj('[name=set_yn]').val();
  if(goods_set_yn != '1'){
    if (state == '') {
      var goodsDtCode = document.getElementById('goodsdt_code').value;
      var goodsDtCount = momoj('#goodsDtCount_' + goodsDtCode).val();
      
      if (typeof goodsDtCount =='undefined' || goodsDtCount == '' ||goodsDtCount == 0) {
        alert('商品已無法訂購');
        return;
      }
    }
  }else{
    if(!isEverySpecSelected(momoj(".InSet"))){
      alert("請選擇商品規格");
      return;
    }
  }

  var cartElements = document.getElementsByName('dely_work');
  var chkCartDelyWork;
  for (var chkCartDely = 0; chkCartDely < cartElements.length; chkCartDely++) {
    if (cartElements[chkCartDely].checked) chkCartDelyWork = cartElements[chkCartDely].value;
  }
  
  // 2012.05.23 fhchen 大型家電入EC倉販售
  if((f.work.value == 'first') && (f.largeMachineYn.value == '1')){
    // 限單1件商品，且商品數量須為1
    if(f.count.value > 1){
      var answer = confirm("提醒您！由於大型家電須獨立結帳，您選擇的此商品數量大於一件，\n系統只會將一件商品放入購物車。\n");
      if(answer){
        f.count.value = 1;
      }else{
        return;
      }
    }
  }

  if(!funcCycleGoods.checkAndAlert())return;//週期購

  //買一送一庫存提示訊息
  var canUseBuy1Get1FreeYn = f.canUseBuy1Get1FreeYn.value;
  if(canUseBuy1Get1FreeYn == '1') {
    var buy1Get1FreeData = {};
    var sel_count = momoj('#count').val();  //購買數量
    if(goods_set_yn == '0') {  //一般商品
      var sel_goodsDtCode = momoj('#goodsdt_code').val();  //客戶選擇商品規格
      var sel_goodsDtStock = momoj('#goodsDtCount_' + sel_goodsDtCode).val();  //商品規格庫存

      if(
          sel_count && !isNaN(sel_count) &&
          sel_goodsDtStock && !isNaN(sel_goodsDtStock)
      ) {
        buy1Get1FreeData = {
            device : 'web',
            goodsCode : momoj('[name=goods_code]').val(),
            setYn : goods_set_yn,
            selCount : sel_count,
            mGoods : {
              mGoodsDtStock : sel_goodsDtStock,
              mCartDtCount : '0'
            }
        };
      }
    }else if(goods_set_yn == '1') {  //SET商品
      var strSetGoodsCode = momoj('[name=setgoods_code]').val();
      if(sel_count && !isNaN(sel_count) && strSetGoodsCode) {
        var arrSetGoodsCode = strSetGoodsCode.split('_');
        if(arrSetGoodsCode && arrSetGoodsCode.length > 0) {
          var setGoodsInfo = {};
          var setGoodsDtStock = {};
          var setCartDtCount = {};
          for(var i = 0; i < arrSetGoodsCode.length; i++) {
            var setKey = arrSetGoodsCode[i];
            var sel_goodsDtCode = momoj('[name=set_' + setKey + '_goodsdt_code]').val();  //客戶選擇SET子商品規格
            var sel_unitQty = momoj('[name=set_' + setKey + '_unit_qty]').val();  //SET子商品單位數量
            if(
                setKey && setKey.length > 3 &&
                sel_goodsDtCode &&
                sel_unitQty && !isNaN(sel_unitQty)
            ) {
              var sel_seq = setKey.substring(0, 3);
              var sel_goodsCode = setKey.substring(3);

              setGoodsInfo[sel_seq + '_' + sel_goodsCode + '#' + sel_goodsDtCode] = sel_unitQty;

              var seGoodsDtStockKey = 'set_' + sel_goodsCode + '_' + sel_goodsDtCode + '_amt';
              var sel_goodsDtStock = momoj('[name="' + seGoodsDtStockKey + '"]').val();
              if(sel_goodsDtStock && !isNaN(sel_goodsDtStock)) {
                setGoodsDtStock[sel_goodsCode + '#' + sel_goodsDtCode] = sel_goodsDtStock;
              }

              setCartDtCount[sel_goodsCode + '#' + sel_goodsDtCode] = '0';
            }
          }

          buy1Get1FreeData = {
              device : 'web',
              goodsCode : momoj('[name=goods_code]').val(),
              setYn : goods_set_yn,
              selCount : sel_count,
              setGoods : {
                setGoodsInfo : setGoodsInfo,
                setGoodsDtStock : setGoodsDtStock,
                setCartDtCount : setCartDtCount
              }
          };
        }
      }
    }
    
    var buy1Get1FreeRtn = momoj.ajaxTool({ data : { buy1Get1FreeData : buy1Get1FreeData, flag : 5009 } });

    if(
        buy1Get1FreeRtn &&
        buy1Get1FreeRtn.rtnCode && buy1Get1FreeRtn.rtnCode == '200' &&
        buy1Get1FreeRtn.rtnData &&
        buy1Get1FreeRtn.rtnData.result && buy1Get1FreeRtn.rtnData.result == '200'
    ) {
      var buy1Get1FreeQtyStatus = buy1Get1FreeRtn.rtnData.buy1Get1FreeQtyStatus;
      var buy1Get1FreeQtyMsg = buy1Get1FreeRtn.rtnData.buy1Get1FreeQtyMsg;
      if(buy1Get1FreeQtyStatus == 'FAIL') {
        alert(buy1Get1FreeQtyMsg);
        return;
      }else if(buy1Get1FreeQtyStatus == 'NO_QTY' || buy1Get1FreeQtyStatus == 'ADJUST_QTY') {
        var ans = confirm(buy1Get1FreeQtyMsg);
        if(!ans) {  //點擊「取消」停留原頁面
          return;
        }
      }
    }else {
      alert('目前系統忙碌中，請稍後再試！');
      return;
    }
  }

  
  var chkIntoCartResult = momoj.runMethod({run:'chkCartGoods',
                                           pa:{goodsCode:'11289042',
                                               delyWork:chkCartDelyWork,
                                               useTwnTraCard:useTwnTraCard,
                                               setYn:'0',
                                               delyTemp:'01',
                                               cartName:f.work.value,
                                               largeMachineYn:'0'
                                               },
                                           js:'//image.momoshop.com.tw/ecm/js/ajaxGoodsTool.js?t=20250730002'
                                           });
  if (chkIntoCartResult.rtnCode == 200) {
    var rtnData = chkIntoCartResult.rtnData;    
    switch (rtnData.resultCode) {
      case '0':
        break;
      case '1':
      case '2':
      case '3':
      case '4':
      case '5':
        var confirmRst = confirm(rtnData.resultMsg);
        if (!confirmRst) {
          return;
        }
        break;
      //檢查是否為廢四機 add by yfchi 2012/03/23
      case '6':
        var _f4g = [
          '<div class="recoverArea">',
          '<p class="mainTxt">「新購公告指定規格之電視機、洗衣機、電冰箱或冷、暖氣機時，販賣業者應提供同項目、數量、',
          '時間及同送達地址之廢四機回收（搬、載運）無償服務。但不包含商用冰箱，為搬運、拆卸而動用大型機具、',
          '工程或危險施工等。請於交付廢四機時向業者索取回收聯單。消費者本人簽名確認已被口頭告知或知悉上述權益。」</p>',
          '<p class="alertTxt">環保署資源回收專線(0800-085717)</p>',
          '<p class="alertTxt">momo購物網消費客戶服務專線：市話直撥4128-200，行動電話請撥02-4128-200</p>',
          '<ul>',
           '<li><a id="recoverY">回收廢四機</a></li>',
           '<li><a id="recoverN">不回收</a></li>',           
          '</ul>',
          '</div>'
        ].join('');
        momoj("#discMachYn").val("1"); //是廢四機!
        var _param = {
          title:'本公司配合環保署廢四機回收服務',
          innerHtml:_f4g,
          boxwidth:700,
          onlyCloseBtn: true
        };
        //浮層
        floatingLayerBox(_param);
        floatingLayerBoxAlignCenter();
        
        momoj("#recoverY").click(function(){
          momoj("#MoMoLM, .floatingLayerBox").remove();
          momoj("#recoverYn").val("1");               
          var firstBuyQty = momoj("#firstBuyQty").val();             
          if (firstBuyQty == "0"){
            submitGoodsDetailForm(goods_code,state);
          } else {
            momoj().MomoLogin({GoCart:false,LoginSuccess:function(){
              checkFirstBuyAjax(goods_code,state);
            }});
          }
        });
        momoj("#recoverN").click(function(){
          momoj("#MoMoLM, .floatingLayerBox").remove();
          momoj("#recoverYn").val("0");
          var recoverYn = momoj("#recoverYn").val();            
          var firstBuyQty = momoj("#firstBuyQty").val();
          if (firstBuyQty == "0"){
            submitGoodsDetailForm(goods_code,state);
          } else {
            momoj().MomoLogin({GoCart:false,LoginSuccess:function(){
              checkFirstBuyAjax(goods_code,state);
            }});
          }
        });
        return;
        break;
      case '7':
      case '8':
      case '9':
      case '10':
      case '11':
        var confirmRst = confirm(rtnData.resultMsg);
        if (!confirmRst) {
          return;
        }
        break;
        default:
        alert('目前系統忙碌中，請稍後再試！');
        return;
    }
  } else {
    alert('目前系統忙碌中，請稍後再試！');
    return;
  }
  
  var firstBuyQty = parseInt(momoj("#firstBuyQty").val());
  var islimitBuy4MemberOnly = momoj("#limitBuy4MemberOnly").val() == '1';
  
  if (firstBuyQty > 0){
    momoj().MomoLogin({GoCart:false,LoginSuccess:function(){
      checkFirstBuyAjax(goods_code,state);
    }});
  }else if(islimitBuy4MemberOnly){
    momoj().MomoLogin({GoCart:false,LoginSuccess:function(){
      submitGoodsDetailForm(goods_code,state);
    }});
  }else if(cycleGoodsInfo.isCycle){ // [週期購]
    var _rtn=momoj.ajaxTool({data:{flag:3039}}); // 3039:登入確認(僅檢查是否登入)
    if(_rtn.rtnCode==200){
      if(_rtn.rtnData.rtnChar=='1'){
        submitGoodsDetailForm(goods_code,state);
      }else{
        alert("請先登入會員，方可使用週期配送服務，謝謝。");
        momoj().MomoLogin({GoCart:false, LoginSuccess:function() {
        submitGoodsDetailForm(goods_code,state);
        }});
      }
    }else{
      alert('目前系統忙碌中，請稍後再試！');
      return;
    }
  } else if(window.isFiveHour) {
    momoj().MomoLogin({GoCart:false,LoginSuccess:function(){
      submitGoodsDetailForm(goods_code,state);
    }});
  } else{
    submitGoodsDetailForm(goods_code,state);
  }
}

var firstBuyIsAlreadySendForm = false;
function checkFirstBuyAjax(goods_code,state){
  if (firstBuyIsAlreadySendForm){
    alert('檢查購物車商品中，請勿重複動作。');
  } else {
  firstBuyIsAlreadySendForm = true;
  var firstBuyAjaxUrl = "/ajax/ajaxTool.jsp?rn=" + Math.random();
  var firstBuySettings = {data:{URL:firstBuyAjaxUrl,flag:5001,goods:11289042}};
  var firstBuyAjaxResult = momoj.ajaxTool({data:firstBuySettings.data});
  firstBuyIsAlreadySendForm = false;
  if (firstBuyAjaxResult.rtnCode == 200) {
    var firstBuyAjaxRtnData = firstBuyAjaxResult.rtnData;
    var firstBuyDesc = firstBuyAjaxRtnData.firstBuyDesc;
    if (firstBuyAjaxRtnData.firstBuyStatus == "S"){
      submitGoodsDetailForm(goods_code,state);
    } else {
      if (firstBuyDesc == "MSG1"){
        alert("請您先登入會員，再將會員禮商品放入購物車中!");
      } else if(firstBuyDesc == "MSG2") {
        alert("很抱歉!本項會員禮商品已經超出活動銷售期間，請您選擇其他會員禮。");
      } else if(firstBuyDesc == "MSG3") {
        alert("會員專屬禮每人限購一次，請您重新確認購物車中是否已經放入本商品!");
      } else if(firstBuyDesc == "MSG4") {
        alert("會員首購禮每人限購一次，請您重新確認購物車中是否已經放入任何首購禮!");
      } else if(firstBuyDesc == "MSG5") {
        alert("很抱歉~您已經購買過本項會員專屬禮了，本項專屬禮每人限購一次!");
      } else if(firstBuyDesc == "MSG6") {
        alert("很抱歉~您不具有本項會員首購禮購買資格!");
      } else if(firstBuyDesc == "MSG7") {
        alert("很抱歉~您已經購買過會員首購禮了，首購禮每人限購一次!");
      } else {
        alert('目前系統忙碌中，請稍後再試！');
      }
      return;
    }
  } else {
    alert('目前系統忙碌中，請稍後再試！');
    return;
  }
  }
}


function toAddGoods(){//加入新版購物車(API)jfchuang 20200102
  switchRtn = true;//是否轉跳新購物車
  var setGoods = new Array();
  var goodsdtCode = momoj("#productForm").find("[name='goodsdt_code']").val();
  //組合商品
  var setYn = momoj("#productForm").find("[name='set_yn']").val();
  if(setYn == '1'){
    goodsdtCode = "000";
    var setgoods_code = momoj("#productForm").find("[name='setgoods_code']").val();
    var setgoodsCodes = setgoods_code.split("_");
    for (var i = 0; i < setgoodsCodes.length; i++) {
      var setGoodsCode = setgoodsCodes[i].trim();
      if(setGoodsCode != ''){
        setGoods.push({"goodsCode": setGoodsCode.substring(3),
                       "goodsdtCode": momoj("#productForm").find("[name=set_"+setGoodsCode+"_goodsdt_code]").val(),
                       "goodsCount": momoj("#productForm").find("[name=set_"+setGoodsCode+"_unit_qty]").val(),
                       "goodsSalePrice": momoj("#productForm").find("[name=set_"+setGoodsCode+"_sale_price]").val(),
                       "setGoodsSeq": setGoodsCode.substring(0,3)
        });        
      }
    }
  }

  
  //NS贈品
  var nsGift = new Array();
  var f = momoj("#productForm");
  if (typeof f.find("[name='gift_goods_code10']").length != 'undefined') {
    var gift_goods_code10s= f.find("[name='gift_goods_code10']");
    var gift_goodsdt_code10s = f.find("[name='gift_goodsdt_code10']");
    var gift_count10s=f.find("[name='gift_count10']");
    for (var i = 0; i < f.find("[name='gift_goods_code10']").length; i++) {
      nsGift.push({"goodsCode": gift_goods_code10s[i].value,//gift_goods_code10
                   "goodsdtCode": gift_goodsdt_code10s[i].value,//gift_goodsdt_code10
                   "goodsCount": gift_count10s[i].value,//gift_count10
                   "goodsSalePrice": 0
      });
    }
  }
  
  //廢四機
  var discMachYn = momoj("#productForm").find("[name='discMachYn']").val();
  var recoverYn = momoj("#productForm").find("[name='recoverYn']").val();
  recoverYn = (discMachYn == '1')?recoverYn:'0';
  
  // 加購品
  var addtionalGoods = new Array();
  var value_arr = momoj("#productForm").find("[name='addgovalue']").val().split(",");
  for (var i = 0; i < value_arr.length; i++) {
    var value = value_arr[i].trim();
    if(value != ''){
      var data_arr = value.split(":");
      if(data_arr.length >= 3) {
        addtionalGoods.push({"goodsCode":data_arr[0],"goodsdtCode":data_arr[1],"goodsCount":data_arr[2]});
      }
    }
  }
  var oc = false; //是否同步未結帳購物車
  var reduceQty = false; //開賣通知扣量
  if(switchRtn){ // 可以前往新車，不執行加入舊車 
    oc = true;
    reduceQty = true;
  }
  var json = {
       cycleFrequency:momoj("#productForm").find("[name='cycle_frequency']").val(),
       cycleTimes:"2", //20200521 wcdeng 週期購移除配送次數，立單時暫時將次數固定為2
       cycleYn: cycleGoodsInfo.isCycle ? "1" : "0",
       goShopCartYn:"1",//是否直接購買，"1"：是，"0"：否
       goods:[
                 {
                 goodsCode:momoj("#productForm").find("[name='goods_code']").val(),
                 goodsdtCode:goodsdtCode,
                 goodsCount:momoj("#productForm").find("[name='count']").val(),
                 work:momoj("#productForm").find("[name='work']").val(),
                 recoverYn: recoverYn,
                 useTwnTraCardYn: momoj("#productForm").find("[name='useTwnTraCard']").val(),
                 wishNo: momoj("#productForm").find("[name='wish_no']").val(),
                 wishGb: momoj("#productForm").find("[name='wish_gb']").val(),
                 addtionalGoods: addtionalGoods,
                 setGoods: setGoods,
                 nsGift: nsGift,
                 applimitBuyYn: "0",
                 applimitBuyfsCode: "",
                 cn: "",
                 defDely: "",
                 limitBuy4MemberYn: momoj("#productForm").find("[name='limitBuy4MemberOnly']").val(),
                 limitBuyQty: momoj("#productForm").find("[name='limitBuyQty']").val(),
                 negativeProfit: momoj("#productForm").find("[name='negativeProfit']").val(),
                 promoNo: "",
                 savegetAmt: "",
                 canUseBuy1Get1FreeYn:momoj("#productForm").find("[name='canUseBuy1Get1FreeYn']").val(),
                 largeMachineMounting:momoj('#largeMachineMounting').prop('checked')?"1":"0", //大家電安裝費
                 largeMachineMountingPromoNo:""
                 }
                ],
       oc:oc,
       reduceQty:reduceQty,
       srcType:momoj("#productForm").find("[name='srcType']").val()?momoj("#productForm").find("[name='srcType']").val():"",
       webCategoryCode:momoj('#cateCode').val(),
       outPlanDate: momoj('#outPlanDate').val(),
       webArea:"",
       //webCategoryCode:momoj("#productForm").find('[name="category_code"]').val(),
       webCid:"",
       webCtype:"",
       webOid:"",
       whCode:momoj("#productForm").find("[name='whCode']").val()?momoj("#productForm").find("[name='whCode']").val():"",
       postalCode:momoj("#productForm").find("[name='postalCode']").val()?momoj("#productForm").find("[name='postalCode']").val():"",
       inputAddress:momoj("#productForm").find("[name='inputAddress']").val()?momoj("#productForm").find("[name='inputAddress']").val():"",
       receiverSeq:momoj("#productForm").find("[name='receiverSeq']").val()?momoj("#productForm").find("[name='receiverSeq']").val():"",
       needInsurance : momoj('#insureChkBox').prop('checked') && momoj('#insureChkBox2').prop('checked')||false //是否同意加購贈險
  };
  
  var rtn = momoj.addGoods(json);
  
  if(!rtn.apiSuccess){
    var _postData = {flag:9001,fun:"GoodsDetail.jsp_toAddGoods",msg:rtn.rtn.resultCode+"/"+rtn.rtn.resultMessage};
    momoj.ajaxTool({data:_postData});
    if(typeof rtn.rtn.resultMessage=="undefined"){
      // 用後端進行執行加入購物車
      var _postData = {flag:3100,data:json};
      var _rtn = momoj.ajaxTool({data:_postData});
      if(_rtn.rtnData.resultCode == '1'){
        return _rtn.rtnData.cartName;
      }else if(_rtn.rtnData.resultMessage != ''){
        alert(_rtn.rtnData.resultMessage+_rtn.rtnData.resultCode);
      }else {
        alert('網路異常，請稍後再試!'+_rtn.rtnData.resultCode);
      }
    }else {
      if(rtn.rtn.resultCode == "SCS135"){
        var delyType = momoj(".shippingList dd").find('input[type=radio]:not(:checked)');
        var delyTypeVal = delyType.attr("value") || '';
        var delyTxt = delyType.attr("delyType") || '';
        delyTxt = delyTxt.replace("-momo出貨","").replace("/離島配送","").replace("-廠商出貨","");
        openfloatingLayerBox4shopcart({
          title: '無法使用超商取貨',
          boxwidth: 450,
          innerHtml: '<div id="singlestoreType1" class="floatingLayerBox recent-address extra-large" style="display: block;"><div class="innerArea"><div class="storeAlertTip"><div class="single-store-content"><p id="singlestoreType1Text" class="text">您已累計兩次(含)以上未取貨，故無法使用超商取貨，請改用其他配送方式。</p></div><div class="btnArea"><a class="gotologin" onclick="clickCancel()" >取消</a><a class="identidy" onclick="rightClick(\''+delyTypeVal+'\')">delyTxt</a></div></div></div></div>',
          id: 'floatingLayerBox'
         });
        momoj(".closeBtn").hide();
        momoj("#floatingLayerBox").css("height","196px");
        momoj("#floatingLayerBox").css("inset","0 0px 0px");
        momoj("#floatingLayerBox .title").css("padding","0px 26px");
        momoj(".identidy").html("改用"+delyTxt);
      }else if(rtn.rtn.resultCode == "SCA025"){
        alert(rtn.rtn.resultMessage);
        var fiveHourAddr = momoj().cookie('fiveHourAddressData');
        var jsonfiveHour = JSON.parse(fiveHourAddr);
        var custNo = getCustNo();
        if(fiveHourAddr){
          var param = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
          param.set("fiveHourYn","1");
          var toFiveHourGoodsURL = window.location.pathname + "?" + param.toString();
          location.replace(toFiveHourGoodsURL);
        }else{
          alert("此為超市快配商品，請先登入或輸入配送地址");
          location.replace('/goods/5hHomepage.jsp');
        }
        return "";
      }else if(rtn.rtn.resultCode == "SCA026"){
        alert(rtn.rtn.resultMessage);
        var param = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        param.delete("fiveHourYn");
        var toNewURL = window.location.pathname + "?" + param.toString();
        location.replace(toNewURL);
        return "";
      } else {
        alert(rtn.rtn.resultMessage);  
      }
      
      if(rtn.rtn.resultCode == "SCS012"){
        location.href = "/main/Main.jsp";
      }
    }
    return "";
  }
  return rtn.rtn.rtnData.cartName;
}

function getCustNo(){
  var ccmedia = momoj().cookie('ccmedia') || '';
  return ccmedia.split('_/')[0].replace('"', '');
}
function clickCancel(){
  momoj('.closeBtn').click();
}

function rightClick(){
  var delyType = momoj(".shippingList dd").find('input[type=radio]:not(:checked)');
  var _buyType = buyType || '';
  momoj('.closeBtn').click();
  
  delyType.click();
  if(_buyType == ''){
    OrderProcess('cart', '');
  }else{
   OrderProcess('cart', _buyType);
  }
}

function submitGoodsDetailForm(goods_code,state){
  var f = document.productForm; 
  var order_method = 'front'; 
  var setYn = momoj('[name="set_yn"]').val();
  if(setYn == '1'){
    momoj('#productForm #goodsdt_code').val('000');//SET品強制給000
  }
  var newShopCartName;
  sendRemarketingAddToCart();

  if (goods_code != '') { 
    var productCode = momoj("#goods_code").val();
    let prePurchaseNotice = getGoodsPrePurchaseNotice(productCode);
    let prePurchaseNoticeData = prePurchaseNotice.rtnData || {};
    if(prePurchaseNoticeData && prePurchaseNoticeData.isShowNotice){//為寵物處方商品
      //開啟浮層
      openPetFoodFloat(prePurchaseNoticeData,goods_code, state);
      return;
    }else{
      putGoodsInCart(goods_code, state);
    }
  } else if ('' == '2') {
    f.action = '/servlet/CartServlet?order_method=' + order_method + '&status=' + state;
    f.target = '';
    f.submit();
  } else {  
    if (f.goodsdt_code.value == '0') {
      alert(momoj.unicode2Str('&#35531;&#36984;&#25799;&#29986;&#21697;&#35215;&#26684;&#65281;'));  
      return false;
    }
    var productCode = momoj("#goods_code").val();
    let prePurchaseNotice = getGoodsPrePurchaseNotice(productCode);
     let prePurchaseNoticeData = prePurchaseNotice.rtnData || {};
    if(prePurchaseNoticeData && prePurchaseNoticeData.isShowNotice){//為寵物處方商品
      //開啟浮層
      openPetFoodFloat(prePurchaseNoticeData , goods_code, state);
      return;
    }else{
      directBuy(state);
    }
  }
}

function openPetFoodFloat(prePurchaseNoticeData ,goods_code , state){
  if(prePurchaseNoticeData){
    var activity = prePurchaseNoticeData.title;
    var shippingMethodContainer = '<div class="content-text">'+ prePurchaseNoticeData.content + '</div>'+
    '<div class="modal-foot">' +
    '  <div class="btn-box">' +
    '    <button id="customButton" class="ec-btn ec-btn-primary btn-close-modal">確定</button>' +
    '  </div>' +
    '</div>';
    openfloatingLayerBoxNoBackgroundClose(activity, shippingMethodContainer, 640);
    momoj("#customButton").on("click",function(){
      clickFloatEnterBtn(goods_code, state);
    });
  }
}

function clickFloatEnterBtn(goods_code, state){
  momoj("#MoMoLM, .floatingLayerBox").remove();
  if(goods_code !=''){//加入購物車btn
    putGoodsInCart(goods_code, state);
  }else{//直接購買btn
    directBuy(state);
  }
}


function directBuy(state) {
  var newShopCartName;
  try{
    newShopCartName = toAddGoods(); // 加入新版購物車(API)
  }catch(e){
    var _postData = {flag:9001,fun:"GoodsDetail.jsp_submitGoodsDetailForm_2",msg:e.toString()};
    momoj.ajaxTool({data:_postData});
    alert("加入購物車失敗!");
  }

  if(switchRtn){ 
    sendGTag(prodInfo);
    if(!!newShopCartName){
      var newCartUrl = shoppingCartApiDomain+"/view/cart/WEB/"+newShopCartName;
      momoj().MomoLogin({GoCart:false, preUrl:newCartUrl, LoginSuccess:function() {
        window.location = newCartUrl;
      }});
    }
    return;
  }
}

function putGoodsInCart(goods_code, state) {
  var newShopCartName;
  try{
    newShopCartName = toAddGoods(); // 加入新版購物車(API)
    if(!!newShopCartName){
      sendGTag(prodInfo);
      alert("加入購物車成功! ");
    }
  }catch(e){
    var _postData = {flag:9001,fun:"GoodsDetail.jsp_submitGoodsDetailForm_1",msg:e.toString()};
    momoj.ajaxTool({data:_postData});
    alert("加入購物車失敗!");
  }
  switchRtn = true;//是否轉跳新購物車
  if(switchRtn){ // 可以前往新車就不加入舊車
    loadSPCart();
    //location.reload();
    return;
  }
}

// 導購再行銷:加入購物車
function sendRemarketingAddToCart() {
  try {
    var remarketingGoodsCode = momoj("#productForm").find("[name='goods_code']").val();
    var remarketingPrice = momoj('.prdPrice li').last().find('span').first().text().replace(/,/g,'');
    var remarketingQuantity = momoj('#count').val();
    var remartketingBrandNo = momoj('input[name=webBrandNo]').val();
    var remartketingGoodsName = momoj('#osmGoodsName').text();
    var categoryID = momoj("#productForm").find('[name="category_code"]').val();
    var custNoForRemarketing = '';
    var emailForRemarketing = '';
    var cookieCcmedia = momoj().cookie('ccmedia');
    if(cookieCcmedia!=null && cookieCcmedia.length>11){
      custNoForRemarketing = cookieCcmedia.substring(0,12);
      emailForRemarketing = 'momo'+custNoForRemarketing+'@fmt.com.tw';
    }
    
    var _mwa_uniVisitorInfo = momoj().cookie('_mwa_uniVisitorInfo');
    _mwa_uniVisitorInfo = _mwa_uniVisitorInfo == null ? '' : _mwa_uniVisitorInfo.slice(0, _mwa_uniVisitorInfo.indexOf("."));
    
    var remarketingCategoriesName = [];
    momoj('#bt_2_layout_NAV').find('ul').find('li').each(function(){
      var _this = momoj(this);
      var cateTmp = _this.text();
      remarketingCategoriesName.push(cateTmp);
    });
    
    // FB
    var pdListForFB = new Array();
    var pdForFB = new Object();
    pdForFB.id = remarketingGoodsCode;
    pdForFB.quantity = parseInt(momoj('#count').val());
    pdForFB.item_price = parseInt(remarketingPrice);
    pdForFB.content_category = momoj("#tempLCode").val();
    pdForFB.brand = momoj("#productForm").find("[name='fullWebBrandName']").val()||'';
    pdForFB.Custom_label_0 = momoj("#productForm").find("[name='entp_code']").val()||'';
    pdListForFB.push(pdForFB);
    fbEnvent('AddToCart', {
      contents: pdListForFB,
      content_type: 'product',
      value: parseInt(momoj('#count').val())*parseInt(remarketingPrice),
      currency: 'TWD'
    });
    
    
    // appier
    var appierItemArray = new Array();
    var appierItem = new Object();
    appierItem.productID = remarketingGoodsCode;
    appierItem.unit = momoj('#count').val();
    appierItem.price = remarketingPrice;
    appierItemArray.push(appierItem);
    window.appier_q = window.appier_q || [];
    window.appier_q.push({"t": "register", "content": { "id": "MkPv", "site": "momoshop.com.tw" }},
      {"t": "type_addcart", "itemList":appierItemArray, "action_id": "bE2EACtU4fUrfQr", "track_id":"72qn3zK802792xc"});
    
    
    // Yahoo
    window.dotq = window.dotq || [];
    window.dotq.push(
    {
      'projectId': '10000',
      'properties': {
        'pixelId': '10018784',
        'qstrings': {
          'et': 'custom',
          'ea': 'AddToCart',
          'product_id': remarketingGoodsCode
        }
    } } );
    
    
    // Criteo
    window.criteo_q = window.criteo_q || [];
    window.criteo_q.push(   
        { event: "setAccount", account: 17930 },
        { event: "setEmail", email: emailForRemarketing },
        { event: "setSiteType", type: "d" },
        { event: "viewBasket", item: [ 
              { id: remarketingGoodsCode, price: remarketingPrice, quantity: remarketingQuantity },
        ]}
    );
    
    
       if(typeof rtbhEventsApi === 'object') {
         rtbhEventsApi.pushOfferId('basketadd', remarketingGoodsCode, emailForRemarketing);
       }
    
    
    //GTM Marco
    var marcoParams = '{' + 
        '"id":"' + remarketingGoodsCode + '", ' + 
        '"name":"' + remartketingGoodsName + '", ' + 
        '"seller":"' + remartketingBrandNo + '", ' + 
        '"quantity":"' + remarketingQuantity + '", ' +
        '"value":"' + remarketingPrice + '", ' +
        '"currency":"TWD"' +
    '}';
    var marcoObject = JSON.parse(marcoParams);
    marcoObject.value = marcoObject.value == null ? 0 : marcoObject.value;
    marcoGTMArray.push(marcoObject);
    window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
    dataLayer.push({
      'event': 'addToCart',
      'Products': marcoGTMArray
    });
    
    momoj().cookie('fromAddToCart', '1');
    momoj().cookie('marcoParams', marcoParams);
    
    
    //GA4
    if(typeof gtag == "function"){
      var ga4CateNameArray = typeof cateNameArray=="undefined"? new Array():cateNameArray;
      var ga4AddToCartProductInfo = [{
        "item_id" : remarketingGoodsCode,
        "item_name" : remartketingGoodsName,
        "price" : remarketingPrice,
        "item_brand" : momoj('.webBrandLink').first().text(),
        "item_category"  : ga4CateNameArray.length>0? ga4CateNameArray[0].trim():'',
        "item_category2" : ga4CateNameArray.length>1? ga4CateNameArray[1].trim():'',
        "item_category3" : ga4CateNameArray.length>2? ga4CateNameArray[2].trim():'',
        "item_category4" : ga4CateNameArray.length>3? ga4CateNameArray[3].trim():'',
        "quantity"       : remarketingQuantity
      }];
      gtag('event', 'add_to_cart', {
        'currency' : 'TWD',
        'items' : ga4AddToCartProductInfo
      });
    }
    
    
    //tenmax埋點 - 加入購物車
    if(typeof sendTenMaxAddToCart == "function"){
      var tenMaxAddToCart = {
        "productId" : remarketingGoodsCode,
        "name"      : remartketingGoodsName,
        "salePrice" : remarketingPrice,
        "quantity"  : remarketingQuantity
      };
      sendTenMaxAddToCart(tenMaxAddToCart);
    }
    //Taboola
    if(typeof _tfa === "object" && typeof taboolaEvents !== 'undefined'){
       taboolaEvents.addToCart([remarketingGoodsCode]);
    }
    
  } catch(e) {
  }
  
  //易觀埋點 - 加入購物車
  'object'===typeof ArkModule&&ArkModule.track&&(
    ArkModule.track('add_to_cart', {
      item_id: remarketingGoodsCode,
      item_name: remartketingGoodsName,
      first_category: remarketingCategoriesName.length > 1 ? remarketingCategoriesName[1] : 'none',
      second_category: remarketingCategoriesName.length > 2 ? remarketingCategoriesName[2] : 'none',
      price2: !remarketingPrice && isNaN(remarketingPrice) ? 0 : parseInt(remarketingPrice, 10),
      item_count2: !remarketingQuantity && isNaN(remarketingQuantity) ? 0 : parseInt(remarketingQuantity, 10)
    })
  );
}

function sendGTag(prodInfo){
  prodInfo.product_quantity = momoj('#count').val();
  //ajax
  var gTagArr = getGTag("addToCart", prodInfo);
  momoj.each(gTagArr,function(k, gTag){
    if(gTag.product_id != undefined){
      // send to google
      console.log("pushing " + gTag.event + ' '+ gTag.product_id + ' ' + gTag.conversion_id + ' ' + gTag.conversion_label + ' ' + gTag.product_value + ' ' + gTag.product_quantity + ' ' + gTag.transaction_id);
      dataLayer.push(gTag);
    } 
  });
}

function StopClick() {
  //  var mediaPlayer = document.getElementById('MediaPlayer');
  var mediaPlayer = momoj('#MediaPlayer');
  var goodsImg = momoj('#goodsimg');
  var videoObj = momoj('video');
  if (goodsImg == 'none') {
    goodsImg.show();
    if (videoObj != null) {
      videoObj.hide();
    }
    if (mediaPlayer != null) {
      mediaPlayer.stop();
    }
    cur_quality='';
  }
}
function trust() {
  momoj(".vendordetailmenu li").removeClass("selected").eq(momoj(".vendordetailmenu li").length-1).addClass("selected");
  momoj(".prdwarp .vendordetailview").hide();
  momoj(".prdwarp .credit").fadeIn("slow");
}


var isInWishList = '0';
function insertWishList(gcode, catcode) {
  if(is18Goods && !isYearAgreeAjax()){//分類頁來的在這判斷18禁
    check18Login();
    return;
  }
  var isEmpPricee = momoj('.prdPrice li').last().text().includes("員工價");
  var goodsPrice = isEmpPricee ? momoj('.prdPrice li').last().prev('li').find('.seoPrice').text().replace(/,/g,'') : momoj('.prdPrice li').last().find('span').text().replace(/,/g,'');
  momoj().MomoLogin({GoCart:false, LoginSuccess:function() {
    momoj.ajax({
      url : "/servlet/MemberCenterServ",
      type : "POST",
      data : {flag:"1054", goods_code:gcode, category_code:catcode, select_yn:isInWishList, goods_price:goodsPrice},
      timeout : 30000,
      success : function(data){
        var obj = data;
        rtnCode = obj.rtnCode;
        var rtnStatus = obj.rtnStatus;

        if (rtnCode == "200") {
          if(rtnStatus == '1') {
            momoj('#addtoTrackingListBtn').attr('src','//img1.momoshop.com.tw/ecm/img/cmm/wishList/addtoTrackingListBtn_done.png');
            momoj('#addtoTrackingListBtn').attr('title','取消追蹤');
            alert("加入追蹤成功！");
            isInWishList = '1';
          } else if(rtnStatus == '2') {
            momoj('#addtoTrackingListBtn').attr('src','//img1.momoshop.com.tw/ecm/img/cmm/wishList/addtoTrackingListBtn.png');
            momoj('#addtoTrackingListBtn').attr('title','加入追蹤清單');
            alert("取消追蹤成功！");
            isInWishList = '0';
          }
        } else if (rtnCode == "EC0001") {
          momoj('#addtoTrackingListBtn').attr('src','//img1.momoshop.com.tw/ecm/img/cmm/wishList/addtoTrackingListBtn.png');       
          alert("已達上限 500 件追蹤商品，請至追蹤清單調整內容後再重新加入追蹤");
        } else {
          console.info("rtnMsg " + obj.rtnMsg);
          alert("很抱歉!伺服器暫時無法連線，請稍候再試，或連繫本公司客服人員處理。");
        }
      },
      error : function(err, msg1, msg2) {
        alert("很抱歉!伺服器暫時無法連線，請稍候再試，或連繫本公司客服人員處理。");
      }
    });
  }});
  
  var goodsDetailCateArray = new Array();
  
  momoj('#bt_2_layout_NAV').find('ul').find('li').each(function(){
    var _this = momoj(this);
    var cateTmp = _this.text();
    goodsDetailCateArray.push(cateTmp);
  });    
  
  
  'object'===typeof ArkModule&&ArkModule.track&&(
    ArkModule.track('add_to_favour', {
      item_id: momoj("#productForm").find("[name='goods_code']").val(),
      item_name: momoj('.prdwarp .prdnoteArea h3').text(),
      first_category: goodsDetailCateArray.length > 1 ? goodsDetailCateArray[1] : 'none',
      second_category: goodsDetailCateArray.length > 2 ? goodsDetailCateArray[2] : 'none',
      price2: !goodsPrice && isNaN(goodsPrice) ? 0 : parseInt(goodsPrice, 10)
    })
  );
}

/** 共用浮層**/
function openfloatingLayerBox(title, innerHtml, boxwidth){
  momoj("body").append("<div class='floatingLayerBox' style='width:" + boxwidth + "px; box-shadow:2px 2px 2px rgba(0,0,0,0.3); overflow:hidden; position:fixed; top:0px; left:0px; bottom:0px; right:0px; margin:auto; z-index:1001'><style>.floatingLayerBox .title .closeBtn::before, .floatingLayerBox .title .closeBtn::after {background-color:#818181; width:24px; height:2px; content:''; margin:-1px 0px 0px -12px; position:absolute; top:50%; left:50%; transform:rotate(45deg); transition:all 200ms ease-out 0s}.floatingLayerBox .title .closeBtn::after {transform:rotate(-45deg)}.floatingLayerBox .title .closeBtn:hover::before {transform:rotate(-45deg)}.floatingLayerBox .title .closeBtn:hover::after {transform:rotate(45deg)}</style><div class='title' style='background-color:#E7E7E7; height:48px; font:bold 16px/22px Helvetica; color:#000000; padding:14px 10px 10px 10px ;box-sizing:border-box;'><b></b><a class='closeBtn' style='width:18px; height:18px; position:absolute; top:15px; right:15px; cursor:pointer'></a></div><div class='innerArea' style='background-color:#FFFFFF; padding:10px 20px'></div></div>");
  //判斷螢幕高度是否小於浮層高度； 若螢幕高度較小，則將高度帶給浮層
  momoj(".floatingLayerBox .innerArea").append(innerHtml);
  momoj(".floatingLayerBox .innerArea").css({"width":momoj(".floatingLayerBox").width(),"padding":"0"});
  if(momoj(".floatingLayerBox .innerArea .prdLists ul li").length >10){
    momoj(".floatingLayerBox .innerArea .prdLists").css({"padding":"20px 0 20px 20px"});
  }
  if(document.documentElement.clientHeight < momoj(".floatingLayerBox .innerArea").height()+48){
    momoj(".floatingLayerBox").css({"max-height":"760px;","height":document.documentElement.clientHeight,"top":(document.documentElement.clientHeight-(momoj(".floatingLayerBox").height()))/2});
    momoj(".floatingLayerBox .innerArea").css({"height":document.documentElement.clientHeight-24});
  }else if(document.documentElement.clientWidth < momoj(".floatingLayerBox").width()){
    momoj(".floatingLayerBox").css({"position":"absolute","right":"auto","bottom":"auto","top":(document.documentElement.clientHeight-(momoj(".floatingLayerBox .innerArea").height()+48))/2});
    momoj(".floatingLayerBox .innerArea").css({"height": momoj(".floatingLayerBox").height()-48,"margin":0});
  }else{
    momoj(".floatingLayerBox").css({"height":(momoj(".floatingLayerBox .innerArea").innerHeight() + momoj(".floatingLayerBox .title").height()+20)});
  }
  momoj(".floatingLayerBox .title b").text(title);
  momoj("body").append("<div id='MoMoLM' style='background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0.3); width:100%; height:100%; position:fixed; top:0px; left:0px; z-index:1000; opacity:1'></div>");
  
  /** 當浮層改變高度時，為了讓浮層固定在正中央，所以當浮層有被點擊時，就去改變浮層style裡的高度 **/
  momoj("body").delegate(".floatingLayerBox","click",function(){
    momoj(".floatingLayerBox").css({"height":(momoj(".floatingLayerBox .innerArea").innerHeight() + momoj(".floatingLayerBox .title").height()+20)});
  });
  /** 關閉浮層與黑透明背景 **/
  momoj("body").delegate("#MoMoLM, .floatingLayerBox .closeBtn","click",function(){
    momoj("#MoMoLM, .floatingLayerBox").remove();
  });
}

function mountFeeGoodsModule(){//安裝費設定模組
  function helper(){
    var url = 'images/installHelp.jpg';
    var title = 'momo';
    var w = '1000'
    var h = '300'
    var opts = {toolbar:0, resizable:0, location:0, menubar:0, status:0};
    var _innerOpts = '';
    if(opts !== null && typeof opts === 'object'){
      for(var p in opts){
        if(opts.hasOwnProperty(p)){
          _innerOpts += p + '=' + opts[p] + ',';
        }
      }
    }
    var dualScreenLeft = window.screenLeft != undefined ? window.screenLeft : screen.left;
    var dualScreenTop = window.screenTop != undefined ? window.screenTop : screen.top;
    var width = window.innerWidth ? window.innerWidth : document.documentElement.clientWidth ? document.documentElement.clientWidth : screen.width;
    var height = window.innerHeight ? window.innerHeight : document.documentElement.clientHeight ? document.documentElement.clientHeight : screen.height;
    var left = ((width / 2) - (w / 2)) + dualScreenLeft;
    var top = ((height / 2) - (h / 2)) + dualScreenTop;
    var newWindow = window.open(url, title, _innerOpts + ' width=' + w + ', height=' + h + ', top=' + top + ', left=' + left);
    if(window.focus){
      newWindow.focus();
    }
  }

  /*
                轉換數字成千分位等等，非純數字則回傳來源數字
    e.g: numberSeparator('99999', 3, ',')  ->  '99,999'
    Params:
    numbers 數字
    digits 位數
    str 轉換字串
  */
  function numberSeparator(numbers, digits, str) {
    if(validateNumber(numbers)) {
      var numbersArray = numbers.split('');
      var result = new Array();
      var count = 0;
      str = str.trim().length == 0 ? ',' : str;
      for(var i = numbersArray.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
        result.unshift(numbersArray[i]);
        if(count == digits - 1 && i > 0){
          result.unshift(str);
          count = 0;
        } else {
          count++;
        }
      }
      return result.join('');
    } else {
      return numbers;
    }
  }

  //檢驗純數字
  function validateNumber(numbers) {
    return numbers.length > 0 && /^[0-9]*$/.test(numbers);
  }

  //設定商品頁加購安裝費
  function setMountFee(){
    var fee = momoj('input#largeMachineMounting').val();
    var quantity = momoj('.prdnoteArea .prdPriceDetail #count').val();
    var result = parseInt(fee, 10) * parseInt(quantity, 10);
    momoj('.installCost span').text(numberSeparator(result.toString(), 3, ','));
  }

  return {
    helper: helper,
    setMountFee: setMountFee
  };
}

var askClickAct = function() {//觸發可訂購時通知我，商品頁。
  var productForm = momoj("#productForm");

  var goodsCode    = productForm.find("[name=goods_code]").val();
  var goodsdtCode  = productForm.find("[name=goodsdt_code]").val();
  var categoryCode = productForm.find("[name=category_code]").val();
  var expectQty    = productForm.find("[name=count]").val();
  var setGoodsDtLt = getSetGoodsDtLt(momoj(".InSet"));

  var rtnData = addRecheckProduct(goodsCode, goodsdtCode, categoryCode, expectQty, setGoodsDtLt);//in ajaxGoodsTool.js

  if(rtnData === "1") {
    alert('已加入補貨通知！(貨到時以Email通知)');
  } else if(rtnData === "2") {
    alert('「補貨通知」清單已有該商品紀錄');
  } else if(rtnData === "3") {
    momoj().MomoLogin({GoCart:false, LoginSuccess:askClickAct});
  } else {
    alert('目前系統忙碌中，請稍後再試！');
  }
};

function checkGoodsInWithList(){
  
  momoj.ajax({
    url : "/servlet/MemberCenterServ",
    type : "POST",
    data : {flag:"4013", goods_code: '11289042'||''},
    timeout : 30000,
    success : function(data){
      var obj = data;
      rtnCode = obj.rtnCode;
      var rtnStatus = obj.rtnStatus;
      if (rtnCode === '200') {
        if(rtnStatus === '0'){
          momoj('#addtoTrackingListBtn').attr('src','//img1.momoshop.com.tw/ecm/img/cmm/wishList/addtoTrackingListBtn.png');
          momoj('#addtoTrackingListBtn').attr('title','加入追蹤清單');
          isInWishList = '0';
        } else if (rtnStatus === '1'){
          momoj('#addtoTrackingListBtn').attr('src','//img1.momoshop.com.tw/ecm/img/cmm/wishList/addtoTrackingListBtn_done.png');
          momoj('#addtoTrackingListBtn').attr('title','取消追蹤');
          isInWishList = '1';
        } 
      } else {
        alert("很抱歉!伺服器暫時無法連線，請稍候再試，或連繫本公司客服人員處理。");
      }
    },
    error : function(err, msg1, msg2) {
      alert("很抱歉!伺服器暫時無法連線，請稍候再試，或連繫本公司客服人員處理。");
    }
  });
}
